    <script>
        $(function(){
            /* handle automatic form expand */
            $('#search-form-text').focus(function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse').collapse('show');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle').toggleClass('collapsed');
            });

            $('#search-form-collapse').on('show.bs.collapse', function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .advanced-text').addClass('hide');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .close-text').removeClass('hide');
            });

            $('#search-form-collapse').on('hide.bs.collapse', function(){
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .advanced-text').removeClass('hide');
                $('#search-form-collapse-toggle .close-text').addClass('hide');
            });

            $('#input-type-all').change(function(){
                if(this.checked){
                    $('#input-type-articles,#input-type-collections,#input-type-videos,#input-type-images,#input-type-documents').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('#input-type-articles,#input-type-collections,#input-type-videos,#input-type-images,#input-type-documents').change(function(){
                if( $('#input-type-all')[0].checked ){
                    $('#input-type-all').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('.input-section-all').change(function(){
                if(this.checked){
                    $('.input-section').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });
            $('.input-section').change(function(){
                if( $('.input-section-all')[0].checked ){
                    $('.input-section-all').prop('checked',false);
                }
            });

            $('#input-d1, #input-d2').datepicker({
                startDate: '-100y',
                format: 'yyyy-mm-dd',
                todayHighlight: true,
                autoclose: 'true'
            }).on('show hide', function(e){
                e.stopPropagation();
            });

            $('#search-form').find('.search-submit').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(){
                $('#search-form').submit();
            });
            

            $('#search-form').on('submit', function(){
                // Filter query
                var sQueryFiltered = $("#search-form input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#search-form input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );
                
                // Define type and section values
                var sTypeVals = $.map($('.input-type:checked'), function(n, i){
                    return n.value;
                }).join(',');
                var sTypeValsSection = $.map($('.input-section:checked'), function(n, i){
                    return n.value;
                }).join(',');
                $('#input-t').val(sTypeVals);
                $('#input-c').val(sTypeValsSection);
                // Scrub empty inputs
                $(this).find(':input').each(function(){
                    if ($(this).val() == '') $(this).attr("disabled", "disabled");
                });
                // Sort by relevance patch
                $(this).find('#select-s option:selected')
                    .filter(function() {
                        return !this.value || $.trim(this.value).length == 0;
                    })
                    .parent()
                    .attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $('#search-form').find('.search-submit').find('[data-fa-i2svg]').replaceWith('<i class="fas tnt-spinner tnt-spin"></i>');
            });
        });
    </script>

<button onclick="topFunction()" id="myBtn" title="Go to top">Top</button><script>
// When the user scrolls down 20px from the top of the document, show the button
window.onscroll = function() {scrollFunction()};

function scrollFunction() {
  if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20) {
    document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "block";
  } else {
    document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "none";
  }
}

// When the user clicks on the button, scroll to the top of the document
function topFunction() {
  document.body.scrollTop = 0;
  document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
}
</script></div><div id="tncms-block-631922" class="tncms-block"><div class="col-md-12 footer-nav">
